! Illegal unit of measure (pt inserted).
<to be read again> 
                   ]
l.212     \includegraphics[width=0.9\textwidth]
                                               {figures/finderpattern3.jpg}
Dimensions can be in units of em, ex, in, pt, pc,
cm, mm, dd, cc, nd, nc, bp, or sp; but yours is a new one!
I'll assume that you meant to say pt, for printer's points.
To recover gracefully from this error, it's best to
delete the erroneous units; e.g., type `2' to delete
two letters. (See Chapter 27 of The TeXbook.)

! Illegal unit of measure (pt inserted).
<to be read again> 
                   ]
l.270     \includegraphics[width=0.9\textwidth]
                                               {figures/alignmentpattern1.jpg}
Dimensions can be in units of em, ex, in, pt, pc,
cm, mm, dd, cc, nd, nc, bp, or sp; but yours is a new one!
I'll assume that you meant to say pt, for printer's points.
To recover gracefully from this error, it's best to
delete the erroneous units; e.g., type `2' to delete
two letters. (See Chapter 27 of The TeXbook.)

! Illegal unit of measure (pt inserted).
<to be read again> 
                   ]
l.283     \includegraphics[width=0.9\textwidth]
                                               {figures/GeoAP.jpg}
Dimensions can be in units of em, ex, in, pt, pc,
cm, mm, dd, cc, nd, nc, bp, or sp; but yours is a new one!
I'll assume that you meant to say pt, for printer's points.
To recover gracefully from this error, it's best to
delete the erroneous units; e.g., type `2' to delete
two letters. (See Chapter 27 of The TeXbook.)

! Illegal unit of measure (pt inserted).
<to be read again> 
                   ]
l.353     \includegraphics[width=0.9\textwidth]
                                               {figures/PersTrans.jpg}
Dimensions can be in units of em, ex, in, pt, pc,
cm, mm, dd, cc, nd, nc, bp, or sp; but yours is a new one!
I'll assume that you meant to say pt, for printer's points.
To recover gracefully from this error, it's best to
delete the erroneous units; e.g., type `2' to delete
two letters. (See Chapter 27 of The TeXbook.)

! Illegal unit of measure (pt inserted).
<to be read again> 
                   ]
l.425     \includegraphics[width=0.9\textwidth]
                                               {figures/QR3.jpg}
Dimensions can be in units of em, ex, in, pt, pc,
cm, mm, dd, cc, nd, nc, bp, or sp; but yours is a new one!
I'll assume that you meant to say pt, for printer's points.
To recover gracefully from this error, it's best to
delete the erroneous units; e.g., type `2' to delete
two letters. (See Chapter 27 of The TeXbook.)
